(function(){
  var track=document.getElementById('wof2Track');
  var dotsWrap=document.getElementById('wof2Dots');
  var counter=document.getElementById('wof2Counter');
  var cards=track.querySelectorAll('.wof2-card');
  var total=cards.length;
  var cur=0;
  var autoTimer=null;
  function buildDots(){
    dotsWrap.innerHTML='';
    for(var i=0;i<total;i++){
      var d=document.createElement('div');
      d.className='wof2-dot'+(i===0?' active':'');
      dotsWrap.appendChild(d);
    }
  }
  function goTo(i){
    cur=((i%total)+total)%total;
    var cardW=cards[0].getBoundingClientRect().width+14;
    track.style.transform='translateX(-'+(cur*cardW)+'px)';
    var dots=dotsWrap.querySelectorAll('.wof2-dot');
    dots.forEach(function(d,j){d.classList.toggle('active',j===cur);});
    counter.textContent=(cur+1)+' / '+total;
  }
  function startAuto(){clearInterval(autoTimer);autoTimer=setInterval(function(){goTo(cur+1);},4200);}
  buildDots();
  startAuto();
  var tx=0;
  track.addEventListener('touchstart',function(e){tx=e.touches[0].clientX;clearInterval(autoTimer);},{passive:true});
  track.addEventListener('touchend',function(e){var df=tx-e.changedTouches[0].clientX;if(Math.abs(df)>38)goTo(df>0?cur+1:cur-1);startAuto();},{passive:true});
  var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
    entries.forEach(function(e){
      if(e.isIntersecting){
        cards.forEach(function(c,i){setTimeout(function(){c.classList.add('vis');},i*70);});
        obs.disconnect();
      }
    });
  },{threshold:0.15});
  obs.observe(document.getElementById('wof2Wrap'));
})();

(function(){
  var items=document.querySelectorAll('#wifItems .wif-item');
  var card=document.getElementById('wifCard');
  var counted=false;

  var obs=new IntersectionObserver(function(e){
    e.forEach(function(en){
      if(en.isIntersecting){en.target.classList.add('wif-in');obs.unobserve(en.target);}
    });
  },{threshold:0.07,rootMargin:'0px 0px -20px 0px'});

  items.forEach(function(el){obs.observe(el);});
  obs.observe(card);

  var cObs=new IntersectionObserver(function(e){
    if(e[0].isIntersecting&&!counted){counted=true;animCount();}
  },{threshold:0.15});
  cObs.observe(card);

  function liveCount(){
    /* Base: 1032 on April 8 2026. Each day adds a seeded-random 2-5. */
    var base=new Date('2026-04-08T00:00:00Z').getTime();
    var days=Math.floor((Date.now()-base)/86400000);
    if(days<=0)return 1032;
    var count=1032;
    for(var d=1;d<=days;d++){
      /* simple seeded hash so same day always gives same number */
      var seed=(d*2654435761)>>>0;
      count+=2+(seed%4); /* 2, 3, 4 or 5 */
    }
    return count;
  }

  function animCount(){
    var target=liveCount(),dur=1800,start=performance.now();
    var el=document.getElementById('wifNum');
    function step(now){
      var p=Math.min((now-start)/dur,1),ease=1-Math.pow(1-p,3);
      el.textContent=Math.floor(ease*target).toLocaleString();
      if(p<1)requestAnimationFrame(step);
      else el.textContent=target.toLocaleString();
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(step);
  }
})();

function mkDots(){
  dt.innerHTML='';
  WGR.forEach(function(_,i){
    var d=document.createElement('button');
    d.className='wgr-dot'+(i===0?' wgr-active':'');
    d.setAttribute('aria-label','Review '+(i+1));
    d.addEventListener('click',function(){goTo(i);});
    dt.appendChild(d);
  });
}
function goTo(i){
  cur=((i%tot)+tot)%tot;
  var w=st.children[0]?st.children[0].getBoundingClientRect().width+16:336;
  st.style.transform='translateX(-'+(cur*w)+'px)';
  var dots=dt.querySelectorAll('.wgr-dot');
  dots.forEach(function(d,j){d.classList.toggle('wgr-active',j===cur);});
}
mkDots();
var tx=0;
st.addEventListener('touchstart',function(e){tx=e.touches[0].clientX;},{passive:true});
st.addEventListener('touchend',function(e){var df=tx-e.changedTouches[0].clientX;if(Math.abs(df)>40)goTo(df>0?cur+1:cur-1);},{passive:true});
setInterval(function(){if(window.innerWidth<=700)goTo(cur+1);},5000);
})();

function mkCard(r){
  var icon=r.platform==='ig'
    ?'<svg width="14" height="14"><use href="#wsr-ig"/></svg>'
    :'<svg width="14" height="14"><use href="#wsr-wa"/></svg>';
  var lbl=r.platform==='ig'?(r.handle?'@'+r.handle:'Instagram'):'WhatsApp';
  return '<div class="wsr-card"><div class="wsr-top"><div class="wsr-av" style="background:'+r.c+'">'+r.in+'</div><div><p class="wsr-name">'+r.name+'</p><p class="wsr-country">'+r.country+'</p></div></div><p class="wsr-text">\u201c'+r.t+'\u201d</p><div class="wsr-foot">'+icon+'<span class="wsr-plabel">'+lbl+'</span></div></div>';
}

document.getElementById('wsrMtrack').innerHTML=html+html;

var dt=document.getElementById('wsrDots');

    d.addEventListener('click',function(){goTo(i);});
    dt.appendChild(d);
  });
}
function goTo(i){
  cur=((i%tot)+tot)%tot;
  var w=st.children[0]?st.children[0].getBoundingClientRect().width+16:336;
  st.style.transform='translateX(-'+(cur*w)+'px)';
  var dots=dt.querySelectorAll('.wsr-dot');
  dots.forEach(function(d,j){d.classList.toggle('wsr-active',j===cur);});
}
mkDots();
var tx=0;
st.addEventListener('touchstart',function(e){tx=e.touches[0].clientX;},{passive:true});
st.addEventListener('touchend',function(e){var df=tx-e.changedTouches[0].clientX;if(Math.abs(df)>40)goTo(df>0?cur+1:cur-1);},{passive:true});
setInterval(function(){if(window.innerWidth<=700)goTo(cur+1);},5500);
})();
